2. Decision Tree Classifier
3. K-Nearest Neighbor Classifier
4. Naive Bayes Classifier - Gaussian or Multinomial
5. Ensemble Model - Random Forest
6. Ensemble Model - XGBoost
For each of the models above, calculate the following evaluation metrics:
1. Accuracy
2. AUC Score
3. Precision
4. Recall
5. F1 Score
6. Matthews Correlation Coefficient (MCC Score)</div></div></div></div></div><div class="z-0 flex justify-end"><div class="touch:-me-2 touch:-ms-3.5 -ms-2.5 -me-1 flex flex-wrap items-center gap-y-4 p-1 <h1 data-start="282" data-end="310">1 logistic_regression.py</h1>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="312" data-end="1728"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">python</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-python"><span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># logistic_regression.py</span></span><span>

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> pandas </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> pd
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> numpy </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> np
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.model_selection </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> train_test_split
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.preprocessing </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> StandardScaler
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.metrics </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> accuracy_score, roc_auc_score, precision_score, recall_score, f1_score, matthews_corrcoef
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.linear_model </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> LogisticRegression

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Load dataset</span></span><span>
df = pd.read_csv(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Pokemon.csv"</span></span><span>)

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Drop non-numeric / irrelevant columns</span></span><span>
df = df.drop(columns=[</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"#"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Name"</span></span><span>], errors=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">'ignore'</span></span><span>)

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Convert categorical columns using one-hot encoding</span></span><span>
df = pd.get_dummies(df, drop_first=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>)

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Define features and target</span></span><span>
X = df.drop(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Legendary"</span></span><span>, axis=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>)
y = df[</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Legendary"</span></span><span>]

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Train-test split</span></span><span>
X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.2</span></span><span>, random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">42</span></span><span>, stratify=y)

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Scale features</span></span><span>
scaler = StandardScaler()
X_train = scaler.fit_transform(X_train)
X_test = scaler.transform(X_test)

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Model</span></span><span>
model = LogisticRegression(max_iter=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">1000</span></span><span>)
model.fit(X_train, y_train)

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Predictions</span></span><span>
y_pred = model.predict(X_test)
y_prob = model.predict_proba(X_test)[:, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>]

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Metrics</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Logistic Regression Results"</span></span><span>)
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Accuracy:"</span></span><span>, accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"AUC:"</span></span><span>, roc_auc_score(y_test, y_prob))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Precision:"</span></span><span>, precision_score(y_test, y_pred))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Recall:"</span></span><span>, recall_score(y_test, y_pred))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"F1 Score:"</span></span><span>, f1_score(y_test, y_pred))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"MCC:"</span></span><span>, matthews_corrcoef(y_test, y_pred))

<h1 data-start="1735" data-end="1768">2 decision_tree_classifier.py</h1>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="1770" data-end="2811"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">python</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-python"><span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># decision_tree_classifier.py</span></span><span>

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> pandas </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> pd
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.model_selection </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> train_test_split
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.metrics </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> accuracy_score, roc_auc_score, precision_score, recall_score, f1_score, matthews_corrcoef
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.tree </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> DecisionTreeClassifier

df = pd.read_csv(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Pokemon.csv"</span></span><span>)
df = df.drop(columns=[</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"#"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Name"</span></span><span>], errors=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">'ignore'</span></span><span>)
df = pd.get_dummies(df, drop_first=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>)

X = df.drop(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Legendary"</span></span><span>, axis=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>)
y = df[</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Legendary"</span></span><span>]

X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.2</span></span><span>, random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">42</span></span><span>, stratify=y)

model = DecisionTreeClassifier(random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">42</span></span><span>)
model.fit(X_train, y_train)

y_pred = model.predict(X_test)
y_prob = model.predict_proba(X_test)[:, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>]

</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Decision Tree Results"</span></span><span>)
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Accuracy:"</span></span><span>, accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"AUC:"</span></span><span>, roc_auc_score(y_test, y_prob))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Precision:"</span></span><span>, precision_score(y_test, y_pred))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Recall:"</span></span><span>, recall_score(y_test, y_pred))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"F1 Score:"</span></span><span>, f1_score(y_test, y_pred))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"MCC:"</span></span><span>, matthews_corrcoef(y_test, y_pred))
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>

<h1 data-start="2818" data-end="2841">3 knn_classifier.py</h1>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="2843" data-end="4013"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">python</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-python"><span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># knn_classifier.py</span></span><span>

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> pandas </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> pd
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.model_selection </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> train_test_split
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.preprocessing </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> StandardScaler
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.metrics </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> accuracy_score, roc_auc_score, precision_score, recall_score, f1_score, matthews_corrcoef
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.neighbors </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> KNeighborsClassifier

df = pd.read_csv(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Pokemon.csv"</span></span><span>)
df = df.drop(columns=[</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"#"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Name"</span></span><span>], errors=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">'ignore'</span></span><span>)
df = pd.get_dummies(df, drop_first=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>)

X = df.drop(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Legendary"</span></span><span>, axis=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>)
y = df[</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Legendary"</span></span><span>]

X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.2</span></span><span>, random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">42</span></span><span>, stratify=y)

scaler = StandardScaler()
X_train = scaler.fit_transform(X_train)
X_test = scaler.transform(X_test)

model = KNeighborsClassifier(n_neighbors=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">5</span></span><span>)
model.fit(X_train, y_train)

y_pred = model.predict(X_test)
y_prob = model.predict_proba(X_test)[:, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>]

</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"KNN Results"</span></span><span>)
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Accuracy:"</span></span><span>, accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"AUC:"</span></span><span>, roc_auc_score(y_test, y_prob))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Precision:"</span></span><span>, precision_score(y_test, y_pred))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Recall:"</span></span><span>, recall_score(y_test, y_pred))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"F1 Score:"</span></span><span>, f1_score(y_test, y_pred))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"MCC:"</span></span><span>, matthews_corrcoef(y_test, y_pred))
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> pandas </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> pd
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.model_selection </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> train_test_split
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.metrics </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> accuracy_score, roc_auc_score, precision_score, recall_score, f1_score, matthews_corrcoef
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.naive_bayes </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> GaussianNB

df = pd.read_csv(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Pokemon.csv"</span></span><span>)

</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Precision:"</span></span><span>, precision_score(y_test, y_pred))

</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"MCC:"</span></span><span>, matthews_corrcoef(y_test, y_pred))

<h1 data-start="5061" data-end="5094">5 random_forest_classifier.py</h1>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="5096" data-end="6159"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">python</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-python"><span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># random_forest_classifier.py</span></span><span>

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> pandas </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> pd
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.model_selection </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> train_test_split
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.metrics </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> accuracy_score, roc_auc_score, precision_score, recall_score, f1_score, matthews_corrcoef
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.ensemble </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> RandomForestClassifier

df = pd.read_csv(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Pokemon.csv"</span></span><span>)
df = df.drop(columns=[</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"#"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Name"</span></span><span>], errors=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">'ignore'</span></span><span>)
df = pd.get_dummies(df, drop_first=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>)

X = df.drop(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Legendary"</span></span><span>, axis=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>)

y_pred = model.predict(X_test)
y_prob = model.predict_proba(X_test)[:, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>]

</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"F1 Score:"</span></span><span>, f1_score(y_test, y_pred))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"MCC:"</span></span><span>, matthews_corrcoef(y_test, y_pred))

<h1 data-start="6166" data-end="6193">6 xgboost_classifier.py</h1>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="6195" data-end="7249"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">python</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-python"><span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># xgboost_classifier.py</span></span><span>

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> pandas </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> pd
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.model_selection </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> train_test_split
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.metrics </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> accuracy_score, roc_auc_score, precision_score, recall_score, f1_score, matthews_corrcoef
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> xgboost </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> XGBClassifier

df = pd.read_csv(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Pokemon.csv"</span></span><span>)
df = df.drop(columns=[</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"#"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Name"</span></span><span>], errors=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">'ignore'</span></span><span>)
df = pd.get_dummies(df, drop_first=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>)

X = df.drop(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Legendary"</span></span><span>, axis=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>)
y = df[</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Legendary"</span></span><span>]

X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.2</span></span><span>, random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">42</span></span><span>, stratify=y)

model = XGBClassifier(use_label_encoder=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">False</span></span><span>, eval_metric=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">'logloss'</span></span><span>, random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">42</span></span><span>)
model.fit(X_train, y_train)

y_pred = model.predict(X_test)
y_prob = model.predict_proba(X_test)[:, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>]

</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"XGBoost Results"</span></span><span>)
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Accuracy:"</span></span><span>, accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"AUC:"</span></span><span>, roc_auc_score(y_test, y_prob))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Precision:"</span></span><span>, precision_score(y_test, y_pred))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Recall:"</span></span><span>, recall_score(y_test, y_pred))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"F1 Score:"</span></span><span>, f1_score(y_test, y_pred))
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"MCC:"</span></span><span>, matthews_corrcoef(y_test, y_pred))
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="7251" data-end="7254">
<h1 data-start="7256" data-end="7272"> Requirements</h1>
<p data-start="7274" data-end="7310">Install required packages if needed:</p>

data-message-id="43a8f78e-4d7f-4d26-b1ac-8035c8c0ccec" dir="auto" class="min-h-8 text-message relative flex w-full flex-col items-end gap-2 text-start break-words whitespace-normal [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-1" data-message-model-slug="gpt-5-2-thinking"><div class="flex w-full flex-col gap-1 empty:hidden first:pt-[1px]"><div class="markdown prose dark:prose-invert w-full wrap-break-word light markdown-new-styling"><pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="0" data-end="12148"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">python</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-python"><span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># app.py</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Streamlit Classification Model Trainer/Evaluator</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Features:</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># a) CSV upload</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># b) Model dropdown (Decision_Tree, KNN, Logistic_Regression, naive_bayes_gaussian, random_forest_classifier, xgboost_classifier)</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># c) Displays metrics (Accuracy, AUC, Precision, Recall, F1, MCC)</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># d) Confusion matrix + Classification report</span></span><span>

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> warnings
warnings.filterwarnings(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"ignore"</span></span><span>)

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> numpy </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> np
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> pandas </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> pd
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> streamlit </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> st

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.model_selection </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> train_test_split
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.preprocessing </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> StandardScaler, label_binarize
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.compose </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> ColumnTransformer
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.pipeline </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> Pipeline
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.impute </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> SimpleImputer

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.metrics </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> (
    accuracy_score,
    roc_auc_score,
    precision_score,
    recall_score,
    f1_score,
    matthews_corrcoef,
    confusion_matrix,
    classification_report,
)

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.linear_model </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> LogisticRegression
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.tree </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> DecisionTreeClassifier
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.neighbors </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> KNeighborsClassifier
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.naive_bayes </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> GaussianNB
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.ensemble </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> RandomForestClassifier

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> matplotlib.pyplot </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> plt

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Optional dependency</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">try</span></span><span>:
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> xgboost </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> XGBClassifier  </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># type: ignore</span></span><span>
    XGBOOST_AVAILABLE = </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">except</span></span><span> Exception:
    XGBOOST_AVAILABLE = </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">False</span></span><span>


MODEL_NAMES = [
    </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Decision_Tree"</span></span><span>,
    </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"KNN"</span></span><span>,
    </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Logistic_Regression"</span></span><span>,
    </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"naive_bayes_gaussian"</span></span><span>,
    </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"random_forest_classifier"</span></span><span>,
    </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"xgboost_classifier"</span></span><span>,
]

DROP_CANDIDATES = [</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"#"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Name"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"ID"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Id"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"index"</span></span><span>]


</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">build_model</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params">model_name: <span class="hljs-built_in">str</span></span></span><span>, scale_numeric: </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">bool</span></span><span>, n_classes: </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">int</span></span><span>):
    <span class="hljs-string">"""
    Returns (estimator, needs_proba) where needs_proba=True means we will compute AUC using predict_proba.
    """</span>
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> model_name == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Decision_Tree"</span></span><span>:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> DecisionTreeClassifier(random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">42</span></span><span>), </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> model_name == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"KNN"</span></span><span>:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># KNN generally benefits from scaling.</span></span><span>
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> KNeighborsClassifier(n_neighbors=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">5</span></span><span>), </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> model_name == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Logistic_Regression"</span></span><span>:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Works for binary and multiclass (softmax).</span></span><span>
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> LogisticRegression(max_iter=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">2000</span></span><span>), </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> model_name == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"naive_bayes_gaussian"</span></span><span>:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># GaussianNB expects dense array; pipeline will output dense.</span></span><span>
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> GaussianNB(), </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> model_name == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"random_forest_classifier"</span></span><span>:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> RandomForestClassifier(n_estimators=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">300</span></span><span>, random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">42</span></span><span>), </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> model_name == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"xgboost_classifier"</span></span><span>:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">not</span></span><span> XGBOOST_AVAILABLE:
            st.error(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"xgboost is not installed in your environment. Install with: pip install xgboost"</span></span><span>)
            st.stop()

        </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Use multi:softprob for multiclass so predict_proba works</span></span><span>
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> n_classes &gt; </span><span><span class="hljs-number">2</span></span><span>:
            clf = XGBClassifier(
                n_estimators=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">500</span></span><span>,
                max_depth=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">4</span></span><span>,
                learning_rate=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.05</span></span><span>,
                subsample=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.9</span></span><span>,
                colsample_bytree=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.9</span></span><span>,
                objective=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"multi:softprob"</span></span><span>,
                num_class=n_classes,
                eval_metric=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"mlogloss"</span></span><span>,
                random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">42</span></span><span>,
            )
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span>:
            clf = XGBClassifier(
                n_estimators=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">500</span></span><span>,
                max_depth=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">4</span></span><span>,
                learning_rate=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.05</span></span><span>,
                subsample=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.9</span></span><span>,
                colsample_bytree=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.9</span></span><span>,
                objective=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"binary:logistic"</span></span><span>,
                eval_metric=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"logloss"</span></span><span>,
                random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">42</span></span><span>,
            )
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> clf, </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">raise</span></span><span> ValueError(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">f"Unknown model: <span class="hljs-subst">{model_name}</span></span></span><span>")


</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">make_preprocessor</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params">X: pd.DataFrame, scale_numeric: <span class="hljs-built_in">bool</span></span></span><span>):
    <span class="hljs-string">"""
    Preprocessing:
      - Drop common ID-like columns if present (handled before call)
      - Impute numeric: median, categorical: most_frequent
      - One-hot encode categorical
      - Optional scaling of numeric (good for KNN/LogReg)
    """</span>
    numeric_cols = X.select_dtypes(include=[</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"number"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"bool"</span></span><span>]).columns.tolist()
    categorical_cols = [c </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span></span><span> c </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> X.columns </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> c </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">not</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> numeric_cols]

    </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Numeric pipeline</span></span><span>
    num_steps = [(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"imputer"</span></span><span>, SimpleImputer(strategy=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"median"</span></span><span>))]
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> scale_numeric:
        num_steps.append((</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"scaler"</span></span><span>, StandardScaler()))
    numeric_transformer = Pipeline(steps=num_steps)

    </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Categorical pipeline</span></span><span>
    cat_transformer = Pipeline(
        steps=[
            (</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"imputer"</span></span><span>, SimpleImputer(strategy=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"most_frequent"</span></span><span>)),
            (</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"onehot"</span></span><span>, OneHotEncoderSafe()),
        ]
    )

    preprocessor = ColumnTransformer(
        transformers=[
            (</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"num"</span></span><span>, numeric_transformer, numeric_cols),
            (</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"cat"</span></span><span>, cat_transformer, categorical_cols),
        ],
        remainder=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"drop"</span></span><span>,
        verbose_feature_names_out=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">False</span></span><span>,
    )
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> preprocessor


</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title class_">OneHotEncoderSafe</span></span><span>:
    <span class="hljs-string">"""
    Lightweight one-hot encoder that returns a dense array and handles unknown categories.
    Implemented to avoid importing sklearn's OneHotEncoder in older environments that sometimes differ.
    If your sklearn supports it, you can replace this class with:
        from sklearn.preprocessing import OneHotEncoder
        OneHotEncoder(handle_unknown="ignore", sparse_output=False)
    """</span>
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">__init__</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params">self</span></span><span>):
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.preprocessing </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> OneHotEncoder
        </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Try newer arg name first, then fallback</span></span><span>
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">try</span></span><span>:
            </span><span><span class="hljs-variable language_">self</span></span><span>.enc = OneHotEncoder(handle_unknown=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"ignore"</span></span><span>, sparse_output=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">False</span></span><span>)
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">except</span></span><span> TypeError:
            </span><span><span class="hljs-variable language_">self</span></span><span>.enc = OneHotEncoder(handle_unknown=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"ignore"</span></span><span>, sparse=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">False</span></span><span>)

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">fit</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params">self, X, y=<span class="hljs-literal">None</span></span></span><span>):
        </span><span><span class="hljs-variable language_">self</span></span><span>.enc.fit(X)
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-variable language_">self</span></span><span>

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">transform</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params">self, X</span></span><span>):
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-variable language_">self</span></span><span>.enc.transform(X)

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">fit_transform</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params">self, X, y=<span class="hljs-literal">None</span></span></span><span>):
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-variable language_">self</span></span><span>.enc.fit_transform(X)

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">get_feature_names_out</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params">self, input_features=<span class="hljs-literal">None</span></span></span><span>):
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-variable language_">self</span></span><span>.enc.get_feature_names_out(input_features)


</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">compute_metrics</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params">y_true, y_pred, y_proba, labels</span></span><span>):
    <span class="hljs-string">"""
    Computes:
      Accuracy, AUC, Precision, Recall, F1, MCC
    AUC:
      - binary: roc_auc_score(y_true, proba[:,1])
      - multiclass: roc_auc_score(y_true_bin, proba, multi_class='ovr', average='macro')
    Precision/Recall/F1:
      - binary: 'binary'
      - multiclass: 'macro'
    """</span>
    n_classes = </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">len</span></span><span>(labels)
    is_binary = n_classes == </span><span><span class="hljs-number">2</span></span><span>

    acc = accuracy_score(y_true, y_pred)

    </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Precision/Recall/F1</span></span><span>
    avg = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"binary"</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> is_binary </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"macro"</span></span><span>
    precision = precision_score(y_true, y_pred, average=avg, zero_division=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0</span></span><span>)
    recall = recall_score(y_true, y_pred, average=avg, zero_division=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0</span></span><span>)
    f1 = f1_score(y_true, y_pred, average=avg, zero_division=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0</span></span><span>)

    mcc = matthews_corrcoef(y_true, y_pred)

    </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># AUC</span></span><span>
    auc = np.nan
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">try</span></span><span>:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> y_proba </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">is</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">not</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">None</span></span><span>:
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> is_binary:
                </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># If proba is shape (n_samples, 2)</span></span><span>
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> y_proba.ndim == </span><span><span class="hljs-number">2</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">and</span></span><span> y_proba.shape[</span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>] &gt;= </span><span><span class="hljs-number">2</span></span><span>:
                    auc = roc_auc_score(y_true, y_proba[:, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>])
                </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span>:
                    auc = roc_auc_score(y_true, y_proba)
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span>:
                y_true_bin = label_binarize(y_true, classes=labels)
                auc = roc_auc_score(y_true_bin, y_proba, multi_class=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"ovr"</span></span><span>, average=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"macro"</span></span><span>)
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">except</span></span><span> Exception:
        auc = np.nan

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> {
        </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Accuracy"</span></span><span>: acc,
        </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"AUC Score"</span></span><span>: auc,
        </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Precision"</span></span><span>: precision,
        </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Recall"</span></span><span>: recall,
        </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"F1 Score"</span></span><span>: f1,
        </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"MCC Score"</span></span><span>: mcc,
    }


</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">plot_confusion_matrix</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params">cm, labels</span></span><span>):
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    im = ax.imshow(cm)
    ax.set_title(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Confusion Matrix"</span></span><span>)
    ax.set_xlabel(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Predicted"</span></span><span>)
    ax.set_ylabel(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Actual"</span></span><span>)

    ax.set_xticks(np.arange(</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">len</span></span><span>(labels)))
    ax.set_yticks(np.arange(</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">len</span></span><span>(labels)))
    ax.set_xticklabels(labels, rotation=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">45</span></span><span>, ha=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"right"</span></span><span>)
    ax.set_yticklabels(labels)

    </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># write values</span></span><span>
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span></span><span> i </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">range</span></span><span>(cm.shape[</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0</span></span><span>]):
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span></span><span> j </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">range</span></span><span>(cm.shape[</span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>]):
            ax.text(j, i, </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">str</span></span><span>(cm[i, j]), ha=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"center"</span></span><span>, va=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"center"</span></span><span>)

    fig.tight_layout()
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> fig


</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># -------------------- Streamlit UI --------------------</span></span><span>
st.set_page_config(page_title=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"ML Classifier Evaluator"</span></span><span>, layout=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"wide"</span></span><span>)
st.title(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">" Classification Models Evaluator (Streamlit)"</span></span><span>)

st.write(
    </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Upload a CSV, choose a target column, select a model, and view evaluation metrics + confusion matrix/report."</span></span><span>
)

uploaded = st.file_uploader(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Upload Dataset (CSV)"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">type</span></span><span>=[</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"csv"</span></span><span>])

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">with</span></span><span> st.sidebar:
    st.header(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">" Settings"</span></span><span>)
    model_name = st.selectbox(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Select Model"</span></span><span>, MODEL_NAMES, index=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0</span></span><span>)
    test_size = st.slider(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Test Size"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.1</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.4</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.2</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.05</span></span><span>)
    random_state = st.number_input(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Random State"</span></span><span>, value=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">42</span></span><span>, step=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>)
    stratify_opt = st.checkbox(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Stratify split (recommended for classification)"</span></span><span>, value=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>)

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> uploaded </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">is</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">None</span></span><span>:
    st.info(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Please upload a CSV to begin."</span></span><span>)
    st.stop()

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Read data</span></span><span>
df = pd.read_csv(uploaded)

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> df.shape[</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0</span></span><span>] &lt; </span><span><span class="hljs-number">10</span></span><span>:
    st.error(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Dataset looks too small for train/test splitting."</span></span><span>)
    st.stop()

st.subheader(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Preview"</span></span><span>)
st.dataframe(df.head(</span><span><span class="hljs-number">20</span></span><span>), use_container_width=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>)

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Suggest default target</span></span><span>
default_target = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Legendary"</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Legendary"</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> df.columns </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span> df.columns[-</span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>]
target_col = st.selectbox(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Select Target Column"</span></span><span>, df.columns.tolist(), index=df.columns.get_loc(default_target))

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Drop likely ID columns if present (except if chosen as target)</span></span><span>
drop_cols = [c </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span></span><span> c </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> DROP_CANDIDATES </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> c </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> df.columns </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">and</span></span><span> c != target_col]
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> drop_cols:
    st.caption(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">f"Dropping likely ID columns: <span class="hljs-subst">{drop_cols}</span></span></span><span>")
    df = df.drop(columns=drop_cols)

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Separate X/y</span></span><span>
X = df.drop(columns=[target_col])
y = df[target_col]

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Handle boolean targets (True/False) and categorical targets</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Convert y to numeric class labels</span></span><span>
y_series = y.copy()
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> y_series.dtype == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"bool"</span></span><span>:
    y_series = y_series.astype(</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">int</span></span><span>)
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span></span><span> y_series.dtype == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"object"</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">or</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">str</span></span><span>(y_series.dtype).startswith(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"category"</span></span><span>):
    y_series = y_series.astype(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"category"</span></span><span>).cat.codes

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># If y is numeric but has missing values, drop rows</span></span><span>
mask = ~pd.isna(y_series)
X = X.loc[mask].reset_index(drop=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>)
y_series = y_series.loc[mask].reset_index(drop=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>)

labels = np.unique(y_series)
n_classes = </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">len</span></span><span>(labels)
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> n_classes &lt; </span><span><span class="hljs-number">2</span></span><span>:
    st.error(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Target column must have at least 2 classes."</span></span><span>)
    st.stop()

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Determine scaling need</span></span><span>
scale_numeric = model_name </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> [</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"KNN"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Logistic_Regression"</span></span><span>]

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Train/test split</span></span><span>
stratify_y = y_series </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> stratify_opt </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">and</span></span><span> n_classes &gt; </span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">None</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">try</span></span><span>:
    X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(
        X, y_series, test_size=test_size, random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">int</span></span><span>(random_state), stratify=stratify_y
    )
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">except</span></span><span> Exception:
    </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># fallback without stratify if stratify fails</span></span><span>
    X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(
        X, y_series, test_size=test_size, random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">int</span></span><span>(random_state)
    )

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Build pipeline</span></span><span>
preprocessor = make_preprocessor(X, scale_numeric=scale_numeric)
clf, needs_proba = build_model(model_name, scale_numeric=scale_numeric, n_classes=n_classes)

pipeline = Pipeline(steps=[(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"preprocess"</span></span><span>, preprocessor), (</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"model"</span></span><span>, clf)])

train_btn = st.button(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">" Train &amp; Evaluate"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">type</span></span><span>=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"primary"</span></span><span>)

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">not</span></span><span> train_btn:
    st.stop()

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Fit</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">with</span></span><span> st.spinner(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Training model..."</span></span><span>):
    pipeline.fit(X_train, y_train)

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Predict</span></span><span>
y_pred = pipeline.predict(X_test)

y_proba = </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">None</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> needs_proba </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">and</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">hasattr</span></span><span>(pipeline, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"predict_proba"</span></span><span>):
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">try</span></span><span>:
        y_proba = pipeline.predict_proba(X_test)
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">except</span></span><span> Exception:
        y_proba = </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">None</span></span><span>

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Metrics</span></span><span>
metrics = compute_metrics(y_test, y_pred, y_proba, labels=labels)

st.subheader(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">" Evaluation Metrics (Test Set)"</span></span><span>)
col1, col2, col3 = st.columns(</span><span><span class="hljs-number">3</span></span><span>)
items = </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">list</span></span><span>(metrics.items())

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span></span><span> i, (k, v) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">enumerate</span></span><span>(items):
    target_col_ui = [col1, col2, col3][i % </span><span><span class="hljs-number">3</span></span><span>]
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">with</span></span><span> target_col_ui:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">isinstance</span></span><span>(v, </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">float</span></span><span>) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">and</span></span><span> np.isnan(v):
            st.metric(k, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"N/A"</span></span><span>)
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span>:
            st.metric(k, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">f"<span class="hljs-subst">{v:<span class="hljs-number">.4</span></span></span></span><span>f}")

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Confusion matrix + classification report</span></span><span>
st.subheader(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">" Confusion Matrix &amp; Classification Report"</span></span><span>)

cm = confusion_matrix(y_test, y_pred, labels=labels)
fig = plot_confusion_matrix(cm, labels=[</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">str</span></span><span>(l) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span></span><span> l </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> labels])

left, right = st.columns([</span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>])

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">with</span></span><span> left:
    st.pyplot(fig, clear_figure=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>)

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">with</span></span><span> right:
    report = classification_report(y_test, y_pred, zero_division=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0</span></span><span>)
    st.text(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Classification Report:\n"</span></span><span> + report)

st.success(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Done!"</span></span><span>)
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="12150" data-end="12171"><strong data-start="12150" data-end="12171">Run it like this:</strong></p>

streamlit run app.py

data-end="12373">Legendary</code></strong> (like your earlier Pokmon dataset), tell me and Ill simplify it to remove the target selector.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="z-0 flex min-h-[46px] [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-1" data-message-model-slug="gpt-5-2"><div class="flex w-full flex-col gap-1 empty:hidden first:pt-[1px]"><div class="markdown prose dark:prose-invert w-full wrap-break-word light markdown-new-styling"><p data-start="0" data-end="137">Running a <strong data-start="10" data-end="47">Streamlit app inside Google Colab</strong> requires a small workaround because Colab does not support normal web servers directly.</p>
<p data-start="139" data-end="198">Below is the <strong data-start="152" data-end="175">step-by-step method</strong> (this works reliably).</p>
<hr data-start="200" data-end="203">
<h1 data-start="205" data-end="243"> Step 1: Install Required Libraries</h1>
<p data-start="245" data-end="270">Run this in a Colab cell:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="272" data-end="324"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">python</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-python"><span><span>!pip install streamlit pyngrok xgboost
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="326" data-end="329">
<h1 data-start="331" data-end="376"> Step 2: Save Your Streamlit App as a File</h1>
<p data-start="378" data-end="417">Create a file called <code data-start="399" data-end="407">app.py</code> in Colab:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="419" data-end="495"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">python</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-python"><span><span>%%writefile app.py
</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Paste your entire Streamlit app code here</span></span><span>
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="497" data-end="579">Paste the full <code data-start="512" data-end="520">app.py</code> code (the one I gave earlier) inside that cell and run it.</p>
<hr data-start="581" data-end="584">
<h1 data-start="586" data-end="629"> Step 3: Run Streamlit with ngrok Tunnel</h1>
<p data-start="631" data-end="714">Colab cannot directly show Streamlit UI, so we create a public URL using <strong data-start="704" data-end="713">ngrok</strong>.</p>
<p data-start="716" data-end="725">Run this:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="727" data-end="1005"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">python</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-python"><span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> pyngrok </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> ngrok

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Kill any existing tunnels</span></span><span>
ngrok.kill()

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Start Streamlit in background</span></span><span>
get_ipython().system_raw(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"streamlit run app.py --server.port 8501 &amp;"</span></span><span>)

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Create public URL</span></span><span>
public_url = ngrok.connect(</span><span><span class="hljs-number">8501</span></span><span>)
</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Streamlit App URL:"</span></span><span>, public_url)
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="1007" data-end="1010">
<h1 data-start="1012" data-end="1047"> Step 4: Click the Generated URL</h1>
<p data-start="1049" data-end="1081">Colab will print something like:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="1083" data-end="1138"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">nginx</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre!"><span><span><span class="hljs-attribute">Streamlit</span></span><span> App URL: http://xxxxxx.ngrok-free.app
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="1140" data-end="1189">Click that link  Your Streamlit app will open </p>
<hr data-start="1191" data-end="1194">
<h1 data-start="1196" data-end="1229"> If ngrok asks for auth token</h1>
<ol data-start="1231" data-end="1349">
<li data-start="1231" data-end="1277">
<p data-start="1234" data-end="1277">Go to: <a data-start="1241" data-end="1275" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="decorated-link" href="https://dashboard.ngrok.com/signup">https://dashboard.ngrok.com/signup<span aria-hidden="true" class="ms-0.5 inline-block align-middle leading-none"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" data-rtl-flip="" class="block h-[0.75em] w-[0.75em] stroke-current stroke-[0.75]"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#304883" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></span></a></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1278" data-end="1302">
<p data-start="1281" data-end="1302">Create free account</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1303" data-end="1327">
<p data-start="1306" data-end="1327">Get your auth token</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1328" data-end="1349">
<p data-start="1331" data-end="1349">Run this in Colab:</p>
</li>
</ol>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="1351" data-end="1408"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">python</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-python"><span><span>!ngrok config add-authtoken YOUR_TOKEN_HERE
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="1410" data-end="1428">Then rerun Step 3.</p>
<hr data-start="1430" data-end="1433">
<h1 data-start="1435" data-end="1455"> Important Notes</h1>
<ul data-start="1457" data-end="1605">
<li data-start="1457" data-end="1507">
<p data-start="1459" data-end="1507">The app runs only while Colab runtime is active.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1508" data-end="1562">
<p data-start="1510" data-end="1562">If runtime disconnects  you must restart Streamlit.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1563" data-end="1605">
<p data-start="1565" data-end="1605">Large datasets may slow down free Colab.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="1607" data-end="1610">
<h1 data-start="1612" data-end="1644"> Alternative (Easier Method)</h1>
<p data-start="1646" data-end="1702">If this is for project submission, I strongly recommend:</p>
<ul data-start="1704" data-end="1862">
<li data-start="1704" data-end="1777">
<p data-start="1706" data-end="1718">Run locally:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="1721" data-end="1777"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">arduino</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre!"><span><span>pip install streamlit
streamlit run app.py
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
</li>
<li data-start="1778" data-end="1862">
<p data-start="1780" data-end="1798">OR deploy free on:</p>
<ul data-start="1801" data-end="1862">

</li>
<li data-start="1854" data-end="1862">
<p data-start="1856" data-end="1862">Render</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="1864" data-end="1897">Its much more stable than Colab.</p>
