<h2 data-start="364" data-end="418"> Colab Cell 2  Write the Streamlit app (<code data-start="409" data-end="417">app.py</code>)</h2>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="419" data-end="9165"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">python</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-python"><span><span>%%writefile app.py
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> warnings
warnings.filterwarnings(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"ignore"</span></span><span>)

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> numpy </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> np
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> pandas </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> pd
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> streamlit </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> st
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> matplotlib.pyplot </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">as</span></span><span> plt

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.model_selection </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> train_test_split
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.compose </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> ColumnTransformer
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.pipeline </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> Pipeline
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.preprocessing </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> StandardScaler, OneHotEncoder, label_binarize
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.impute </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> SimpleImputer

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.metrics </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> (
    accuracy_score, roc_auc_score, precision_score, recall_score, f1_score,
    matthews_corrcoef, confusion_matrix, classification_report
)

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.linear_model </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> LogisticRegression
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.tree </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> DecisionTreeClassifier
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.neighbors </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> KNeighborsClassifier
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.naive_bayes </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> GaussianNB
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> sklearn.ensemble </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> RandomForestClassifier

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Optional: XGBoost</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">try</span></span><span>:
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span></span><span> xgboost </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span></span><span> XGBClassifier
    XGBOOST_AVAILABLE = </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">except</span></span><span> Exception:
    XGBOOST_AVAILABLE = </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">False</span></span><span>


MODEL_NAMES = [
    </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Decision_Tree"</span></span><span>,
    </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"KNN"</span></span><span>,
    </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Logistic_Regression"</span></span><span>,
    </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"naive_bayes_gaussian"</span></span><span>,
    </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"random_forest_classifier"</span></span><span>,
    </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"xgboost_classifier"</span></span><span>,
]

DROP_CANDIDATES = [</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"#"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Name"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"ID"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Id"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"index"</span></span><span>]


</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">build_model</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params">model_name: <span class="hljs-built_in">str</span></span></span><span>, n_classes: </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">int</span></span><span>):
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> model_name == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Decision_Tree"</span></span><span>:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> DecisionTreeClassifier(random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">42</span></span><span>)

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> model_name == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"KNN"</span></span><span>:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> KNeighborsClassifier(n_neighbors=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">5</span></span><span>)

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> model_name == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Logistic_Regression"</span></span><span>:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> LogisticRegression(max_iter=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">2000</span></span><span>)

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> model_name == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"naive_bayes_gaussian"</span></span><span>:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> GaussianNB()

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> model_name == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"random_forest_classifier"</span></span><span>:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> RandomForestClassifier(n_estimators=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">300</span></span><span>, random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">42</span></span><span>)

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> model_name == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"xgboost_classifier"</span></span><span>:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">not</span></span><span> XGBOOST_AVAILABLE:
            st.error(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"xgboost is not installed. In Colab: pip install xgboost"</span></span><span>)
            st.stop()

        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> n_classes &gt; </span><span><span class="hljs-number">2</span></span><span>:
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> XGBClassifier(
                n_estimators=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">500</span></span><span>,
                max_depth=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">4</span></span><span>,
                learning_rate=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.05</span></span><span>,
                subsample=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.9</span></span><span>,
                colsample_bytree=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.9</span></span><span>,
                objective=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"multi:softprob"</span></span><span>,
                num_class=n_classes,
                eval_metric=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"mlogloss"</span></span><span>,
                random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">42</span></span><span>,
            )
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span>:
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> XGBClassifier(
                n_estimators=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">500</span></span><span>,
                max_depth=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">4</span></span><span>,
                learning_rate=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.05</span></span><span>,
                subsample=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.9</span></span><span>,
                colsample_bytree=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.9</span></span><span>,
                objective=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"binary:logistic"</span></span><span>,
                eval_metric=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"logloss"</span></span><span>,
                random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">42</span></span><span>,
            )

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">raise</span></span><span> ValueError(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Unknown model selected"</span></span><span>)


</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">make_preprocessor</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params">X: pd.DataFrame, scale_numeric: <span class="hljs-built_in">bool</span></span></span><span>):
    numeric_cols = X.select_dtypes(include=[</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"number"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"bool"</span></span><span>]).columns.tolist()
    categorical_cols = [c </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span></span><span> c </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> X.columns </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> c </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">not</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> numeric_cols]

    num_steps = [(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"imputer"</span></span><span>, SimpleImputer(strategy=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"median"</span></span><span>))]
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> scale_numeric:
        num_steps.append((</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"scaler"</span></span><span>, StandardScaler()))
    numeric_transformer = Pipeline(steps=num_steps)

    cat_transformer = Pipeline(
        steps=[
            (</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"imputer"</span></span><span>, SimpleImputer(strategy=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"most_frequent"</span></span><span>)),
            </span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Return dense output for compatibility in Colab</span></span><span>
            (</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"onehot"</span></span><span>, OneHotEncoder(handle_unknown=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"ignore"</span></span><span>, sparse=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">False</span></span><span>)),
        ]
    )

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> ColumnTransformer(
        transformers=[
            (</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"num"</span></span><span>, numeric_transformer, numeric_cols),
            (</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"cat"</span></span><span>, cat_transformer, categorical_cols),
        ],
        remainder=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"drop"</span></span><span>,
    )


</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">compute_metrics</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params">y_true, y_pred, y_proba, labels</span></span><span>):
    n_classes = </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">len</span></span><span>(labels)
    is_binary = (n_classes == </span><span><span class="hljs-number">2</span></span><span>)

    acc = accuracy_score(y_true, y_pred)
    avg = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"binary"</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> is_binary </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"macro"</span></span><span>

    prec = precision_score(y_true, y_pred, average=avg, zero_division=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0</span></span><span>)
    rec = recall_score(y_true, y_pred, average=avg, zero_division=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0</span></span><span>)
    f1 = f1_score(y_true, y_pred, average=avg, zero_division=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0</span></span><span>)
    mcc = matthews_corrcoef(y_true, y_pred)

    auc = np.nan
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">try</span></span><span>:
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> y_proba </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">is</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">not</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">None</span></span><span>:
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> is_binary:
                auc = roc_auc_score(y_true, y_proba[:, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>])
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span>:
                y_true_bin = label_binarize(y_true, classes=labels)
                auc = roc_auc_score(y_true_bin, y_proba, multi_class=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"ovr"</span></span><span>, average=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"macro"</span></span><span>)
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">except</span></span><span> Exception:
        auc = np.nan

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> {
        </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Accuracy"</span></span><span>: acc,
        </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"AUC Score"</span></span><span>: auc,
        </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Precision"</span></span><span>: prec,
        </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Recall"</span></span><span>: rec,
        </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"F1 Score"</span></span><span>: f1,
        </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"MCC Score"</span></span><span>: mcc,
    }


</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-title function_">plot_cm</span></span><span>(</span><span><span class="hljs-params">cm, labels</span></span><span>):
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    ax.imshow(cm)
    ax.set_title(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Confusion Matrix"</span></span><span>)
    ax.set_xlabel(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Predicted"</span></span><span>)
    ax.set_ylabel(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Actual"</span></span><span>)
    ax.set_xticks(np.arange(</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">len</span></span><span>(labels)))
    ax.set_yticks(np.arange(</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">len</span></span><span>(labels)))
    ax.set_xticklabels(labels, rotation=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">45</span></span><span>, ha=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"right"</span></span><span>)
    ax.set_yticklabels(labels)

    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span></span><span> i </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">range</span></span><span>(cm.shape[</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0</span></span><span>]):
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span></span><span> j </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">range</span></span><span>(cm.shape[</span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>]):
            ax.text(j, i, </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">str</span></span><span>(cm[i, j]), ha=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"center"</span></span><span>, va=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"center"</span></span><span>)

    fig.tight_layout()
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">return</span></span><span> fig


</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># ---------------- Streamlit UI ----------------</span></span><span>
st.set_page_config(page_title=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Colab-Friendly Classifier Evaluator"</span></span><span>, layout=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"wide"</span></span><span>)
st.title(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">" Colab-Friendly ML Classifier Evaluator"</span></span><span>)

st.markdown(
    <span class="hljs-string">"""
**Features**
- Upload CSV dataset
- Select target column
- Choose model from dropdown
- View metrics + confusion matrix + classification report
"""</span>
)

uploaded = st.file_uploader(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Upload Dataset (CSV)"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">type</span></span><span>=[</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"csv"</span></span><span>])

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">with</span></span><span> st.sidebar:
    st.header(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">" Settings"</span></span><span>)
    model_name = st.selectbox(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Model"</span></span><span>, MODEL_NAMES)
    test_size = st.slider(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Test Size"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.1</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.4</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.2</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">0.05</span></span><span>)
    random_state = st.number_input(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Random State"</span></span><span>, value=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">42</span></span><span>, step=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>)
    stratify_opt = st.checkbox(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Stratify split"</span></span><span>, value=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>)

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> uploaded </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">is</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">None</span></span><span>:
    st.info(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Upload a CSV file to start."</span></span><span>)
    st.stop()

df = pd.read_csv(uploaded)

st.subheader(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Dataset preview"</span></span><span>)
st.dataframe(df.head(</span><span><span class="hljs-number">20</span></span><span>), use_container_width=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>)

default_target = </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Legendary"</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Legendary"</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> df.columns </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span> df.columns[-</span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>]
target_col = st.selectbox(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Target column"</span></span><span>, df.columns.tolist(), index=df.columns.get_loc(default_target))

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Drop likely ID columns (but never drop target)</span></span><span>
drop_cols = [c </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span></span><span> c </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> DROP_CANDIDATES </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> c </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> df.columns </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">and</span></span><span> c != target_col]
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> drop_cols:
    st.caption(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">f"Dropping ID-like columns: <span class="hljs-subst">{drop_cols}</span></span></span><span>")
    df = df.drop(columns=drop_cols)

X = df.drop(columns=[target_col])
y = df[target_col]

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Convert y to numeric codes if categorical</span></span><span>
y_series = y.copy()
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> y_series.dtype == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"bool"</span></span><span>:
    y_series = y_series.astype(</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">int</span></span><span>)
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">elif</span></span><span> y_series.dtype == </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"object"</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">or</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">str</span></span><span>(y_series.dtype).startswith(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"category"</span></span><span>):
    y_series = y_series.astype(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"category"</span></span><span>).cat.codes

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Drop rows with missing target</span></span><span>
mask = ~pd.isna(y_series)
X = X.loc[mask].reset_index(drop=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>)
y_series = y_series.loc[mask].reset_index(drop=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>)

labels = np.unique(y_series)
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">len</span></span><span>(labels) &lt; </span><span><span class="hljs-number">2</span></span><span>:
    st.error(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Target must have at least 2 classes."</span></span><span>)
    st.stop()

</span><span><span class="hljs-comment"># Scaling for models that benefit from it</span></span><span>
scale_numeric = model_name </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> [</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"KNN"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Logistic_Regression"</span></span><span>]

stratify_y = y_series </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> stratify_opt </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">None</span></span><span>
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">try</span></span><span>:
    X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(
        X, y_series, test_size=test_size, random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">int</span></span><span>(random_state), stratify=stratify_y
    )
</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">except</span></span><span> Exception:
    X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(
        X, y_series, test_size=test_size, random_state=</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">int</span></span><span>(random_state)
    )

preprocessor = make_preprocessor(X, scale_numeric=scale_numeric)
clf = build_model(model_name, n_classes=</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">len</span></span><span>(labels))
pipe = Pipeline([(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"preprocess"</span></span><span>, preprocessor), (</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"model"</span></span><span>, clf)])

</span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> st.button(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">" Train &amp; Evaluate"</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">type</span></span><span>=</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"primary"</span></span><span>):
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">with</span></span><span> st.spinner(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Training..."</span></span><span>):
        pipe.fit(X_train, y_train)

    y_pred = pipe.predict(X_test)

    y_proba = </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">None</span></span><span>
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">hasattr</span></span><span>(pipe, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"predict_proba"</span></span><span>):
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">try</span></span><span>:
            y_proba = pipe.predict_proba(X_test)
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">except</span></span><span> Exception:
            y_proba = </span><span><span class="hljs-literal">None</span></span><span>

    metrics = compute_metrics(y_test, y_pred, y_proba, labels)

    st.subheader(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">" Evaluation Metrics (Test Set)"</span></span><span>)
    mcols = st.columns(</span><span><span class="hljs-number">3</span></span><span>)
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span></span><span> i, (k, v) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">enumerate</span></span><span>(metrics.items()):
        </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">with</span></span><span> mcols[i % </span><span><span class="hljs-number">3</span></span><span>]:
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">if</span></span><span> </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">isinstance</span></span><span>(v, </span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">float</span></span><span>) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">and</span></span><span> np.isnan(v):
                st.metric(k, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"N/A"</span></span><span>)
            </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">else</span></span><span>:
                st.metric(k, </span><span><span class="hljs-string">f"<span class="hljs-subst">{v:<span class="hljs-number">.4</span></span></span></span><span>f}")

    st.subheader(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">" Confusion Matrix &amp; Classification Report"</span></span><span>)
    cm = confusion_matrix(y_test, y_pred, labels=labels)
    fig = plot_cm(cm, [</span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">str</span></span><span>(l) </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">for</span></span><span> l </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">in</span></span><span> labels])

    left, right = st.columns([</span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>, </span><span><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span><span>])
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">with</span></span><span> left:
        st.pyplot(fig, clear_figure=</span><span><span class="hljs-literal">True</span></span><span>)
    </span><span><span class="hljs-keyword">with</span></span><span> right:
        st.text(classification_report(y_test, y_pred, zero_division=</span><span><span class="hljs-number">0</span></span><span>))

    st.success(</span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Done!"</span></span><span>)
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>

)

time.sleep(</span><span><span class="hljs-number">2</span></span><span>)

px-(--thread-content-margin)"><div class="[--thread-content-max-width:40rem] @w-lg/main:[--thread-content-max-width:48rem] mx-auto max-w-(--thread-content-max-width) flex-1 group/turn-messages [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-1" data-message-model-slug="gpt-5-2"><div class="flex w-full flex-col gap-1 empty:hidden first:pt-[1px]"><div class="markdown prose dark:prose-invert w-full wrap-break-word light markdown-new-styling"><p data-start="0" data-end="97">Here are the different ways to create a <strong data-start="40" data-end="67"><code data-start="42" data-end="48">main</code> branch in GitHub</strong>, depending on your situation.</p>
<hr data-start="99" data-end="102">
<h1 data-start="104" data-end="179"> Case 1: Create <code data-start="123" data-end="129">main</code> branch in a NEW repository (using GitHub website)</h1>
<ol data-start="181" data-end="333">
<li data-start="181" data-end="217">
<p data-start="184" data-end="217">Go to <strong data-start="190" data-end="217">GitHub  New Repository</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="218" data-end="242">
<p data-start="221" data-end="242">Enter repository name</p>
</li>
<li data-start="243" data-end="302">
<p data-start="246" data-end="256">Make sure:</p>
<ul data-start="260" data-end="302">
<li data-start="260" data-end="302">
<p data-start="262" data-end="302"> Initialize with README is checked</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="303" data-end="333">
<p data-start="306" data-end="333">Click <strong data-start="312" data-end="333">Create repository</strong></p>
</li>
</ol>
<p data-start="335" data-end="381">By default, GitHub now creates a branch named:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="383" data-end="395"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">css</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre!"><span><span><span class="hljs-selector-tag">main</span></span><span>
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="397" data-end="404"> Done.</p>
<hr data-start="406" data-end="409">
<h1 data-start="411" data-end="485"> Case 2: You already have a repo but no <code data-start="454" data-end="460">main</code> branch (using GitHub UI)</h1>
<p data-start="487" data-end="534">If your repo has <code data-start="504" data-end="512">master</code> or some other branch:</p>
<ol data-start="536" data-end="668">
<li data-start="536" data-end="560">
<p data-start="539" data-end="560">Go to your repository</p>
</li>
<li data-start="561" data-end="604">
<p data-start="564" data-end="604">Click the <strong data-start="574" data-end="593">Branch dropdown</strong> (top-left)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="605" data-end="635">
<p data-start="608" data-end="613">Type:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="617" data-end="635"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">css</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre!"><span><span><span class="hljs-selector-tag">main</span></span><span>
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
</li>
<li data-start="636" data-end="668">
<p data-start="639" data-end="668">Click <strong data-start="645" data-end="668">Create branch: main</strong></p>
</li>
</ol>
<p data-start="670" data-end="699">Now you have a <code data-start="685" data-end="691">main</code> branch.</p>
<hr data-start="701" data-end="704">
<h1 data-start="706" data-end="764"> Case 3: Create <code data-start="725" data-end="731">main</code> branch using Git (Local Machine)</h1>
<p data-start="766" data-end="792">If you're working locally:</p>
<h3 data-start="794" data-end="827">Step 1  Check current branch</h3>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="828" data-end="850"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span>git branch
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<h3 data-start="852" data-end="883">Step 2  Create main branch</h3>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="884" data-end="916"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span>git checkout -b main
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<h3 data-start="918" data-end="948">Step 3  Push it to GitHub</h3>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="949" data-end="984"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span>git push -u origin main
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="986" data-end="989">
<h1 data-start="991" data-end="1041"> Case 4: Rename existing branch (master  main)</h1>
<p data-start="1043" data-end="1078">If your current branch is <code data-start="1069" data-end="1077">master</code>:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="1080" data-end="1141"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span>git branch -m master main
git push -u origin main
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="1143" data-end="1177">Then delete old branch (optional):</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="1179" data-end="1222"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span>git push origin --delete master
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="1224" data-end="1227">
<h1 data-start="1229" data-end="1273"> Set <code data-start="1237" data-end="1243">main</code> as Default Branch (Important)</h1>
<ol data-start="1275" data-end="1396">
<li data-start="1275" data-end="1305">
<p data-start="1278" data-end="1305">Go to <strong data-start="1284" data-end="1305">GitHub repository</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1306" data-end="1327">
<p data-start="1309" data-end="1327">Click <strong data-start="1315" data-end="1327">Settings</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1328" data-end="1349">
<p data-start="1331" data-end="1349">Click <strong data-start="1337" data-end="1349">Branches</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1350" data-end="1388">
<p data-start="1353" data-end="1388">Change <strong data-start="1360" data-end="1378">Default branch</strong> to <code data-start="1382" data-end="1388">main</code></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1389" data-end="1396">
<p data-start="1392" data-end="1396">Save</p>
</li>
</ol>
<hr data-start="1398" data-end="1401">
<h1 data-start="1403" data-end="1428"> Check if main exists</h1>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="1430" data-end="1452"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span>git branch
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="1454" data-end="1496">or on GitHub website, see branch dropdown.</p>
<hr data-start="1498" data-end="1501">
<h1 data-start="1503" data-end="1544"> Most Common Commands (Quick Version)</h1>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="1546" data-end="1602"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span>git checkout -b main
git push -u origin main
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>

light markdown-new-styling"><p data-start="0" data-end="100">Heres a <strong data-start="9" data-end="37">clear step-by-step guide</strong> to push a folder and files to the <strong data-start="72" data-end="99"><code data-start="74" data-end="80">main</code> branch on GitHub</strong>.</p>
<hr data-start="102" data-end="105">
<h1 data-start="107" data-end="165"> Method 1: Push Existing Folder to GitHub (Most Common)</h1>
<h2 data-start="167" data-end="211"> Step 1: Open Terminal / Command Prompt</h2>
<p data-start="213" data-end="245">Navigate to your project folder:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="247" data-end="289"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">cd</span></span><span> path/to/your/project_folder
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="291" data-end="294">
<h2 data-start="296" data-end="341"> Step 2: Initialize Git (if not already)</h2>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="343" data-end="363"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span>git init
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="365" data-end="368">
<h2 data-start="370" data-end="405"> Step 3: Add Remote Repository</h2>
<p data-start="407" data-end="456">Create a repository on GitHub first (empty repo).</p>
<p data-start="458" data-end="489">Then copy the repo URL and run:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="491" data-end="576"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span>git remote add origin https://github.com/your-username/your-repo-name.git
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="578" data-end="584">Check:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="586" data-end="611"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span>git remote -v
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="613" data-end="616">
<h2 data-start="618" data-end="665"> Step 4: Create or Switch to <code data-start="652" data-end="658">main</code> Branch</h2>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="667" data-end="699"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span>git checkout -b main
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="701" data-end="726">If <code data-start="704" data-end="710">main</code> already exists:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="728" data-end="757"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span>git checkout main
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="759" data-end="762">
<h2 data-start="764" data-end="791"> Step 5: Add All Files</h2>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="793" data-end="814"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span>git add .
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="816" data-end="848">To check what will be committed:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="850" data-end="872"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span>git status
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="874" data-end="877">
<h2 data-start="879" data-end="905"> Step 6: Commit Files</h2>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="907" data-end="949"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span>git commit -m </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"Initial commit"</span></span><span>
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="951" data-end="954">
<h2 data-start="956" data-end="991"> Step 7: Push to GitHub <code data-start="985" data-end="991">main</code></h2>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="993" data-end="1028"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span>git push -u origin main
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="1030" data-end="1094"> Now your folder and all files are pushed to the <code data-start="1080" data-end="1086">main</code> branch.</p>
<hr data-start="1096" data-end="1099">
<h1 data-start="1101" data-end="1151"> If Repository Already Has Files (Like README)</h1>
<p data-start="1153" data-end="1186">If GitHub repo is not empty, use:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="1188" data-end="1272"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span>git pull origin main --allow-unrelated-histories
git push -u origin main
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="1274" data-end="1277">
<h1 data-start="1279" data-end="1308"> Quick All-in-One Version</h1>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="1310" data-end="1496"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">bash</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-bash"><span><span><span class="hljs-built_in">cd</span></span><span> your_project_folder
git init
git remote add origin https://github.com/username/repo.git
git checkout -b main
git add .
git commit -m </span><span><span class="hljs-string">"First commit"</span></span><span>
git push -u origin main
</span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="1498" data-end="1501">
<h1 data-start="1503" data-end="1539"> If You Get Authentication Error</h1>
<p data-start="1541" data-end="1613">GitHub now requires <strong data-start="1561" data-end="1592">Personal Access Token (PAT)</strong> instead of password.</p>
<ol data-start="1615" data-end="1760">
<li data-start="1615" data-end="1689">
<p data-start="1618" data-end="1689">Go to GitHub  Settings  Developer Settings  Personal Access Tokens</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1690" data-end="1713">
<p data-start="1693" data-end="1713">Generate new token</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1714" data-end="1760">
<p data-start="1717" data-end="1760">Use token instead of password when prompted</p>
</li>
</ol>
<hr data-start="1762" data-end="1765">
<h1 data-start="1767" data-end="1794"> Check Branch on GitHub</h1>
<p data-start="1796" data-end="1859">Go to your repository  Branch dropdown  Ensure <code data-start="1845" data-end="1851">main</code> exists.</p>

<h1 data-start="267" data-end="297"> Step 2: Create <code data-start="286" data-end="297">README.md</code></h1>
<p data-start="299" data-end="359">Create a file named <strong data-start="319" data-end="334"><code data-start="321" data-end="332">README.md</code></strong> and paste the following:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="361" data-end="3143"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl corner-superellipse/1.1 relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary select-none rounded-t-2xl corner-t-superellipse/1.1">markdown</div><div class="sticky top-[calc(var(--sticky-padding-top)+9*var(--spacing))]"><div class="absolute end-0 bottom-0 flex h-9 items-center pe-2"><div class="bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary text-token-text-secondary flex items-center gap-4 rounded-sm px-2 font-sans text-xs"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1" aria-label="Copy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-gvfid0kn.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>Copy code</button></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-markdown"><span><span><span class="hljs-section"># Classification Models on Pokemon Dataset</span></span><span>

</span><span><span class="hljs-section">## a. Problem Statement</span></span><span>
The objective of this project is to implement and compare multiple supervised machine learning classification models on the same dataset. 

The models are evaluated using the following performance metrics:
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Accuracy
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> AUC Score
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Precision
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Recall
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> F1 Score
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Matthews Correlation Coefficient (MCC)

A Streamlit app is also developed to:
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Upload dataset (CSV)
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Select model
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Train model
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Display evaluation metrics
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Display confusion matrix / classification report

---

</span><span><span class="hljs-section">## b. Dataset Description [1 Mark]</span></span><span>

Dataset: Pokemon.csv  

The dataset contains information about different Pokmon characters including:
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> HP
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Attack
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Defense
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Special Attack
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Special Defense
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Speed
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Type (categorical)
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Legendary (Target variable)

Target Variable:
Legendary (Binary Classification: True / False)

Preprocessing steps:
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Dropped non-informative columns (e.g., #, Name)
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> One-hot encoding for categorical variables
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> 80/20 Train-Test split
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">-</span></span><span> Feature scaling for Logistic Regression and KNN

---

</span><span><span class="hljs-section">## c. Models Used [6 Marks]</span></span><span>

The following 6 classification models were implemented:

</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">1.</span></span><span> Logistic Regression  
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">2.</span></span><span> Decision Tree Classifier  
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">3.</span></span><span> K-Nearest Neighbor (kNN)  
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">4.</span></span><span> Naive Bayes (Gaussian)  
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">5.</span></span><span> Random Forest (Ensemble)  
</span><span><span class="hljs-bullet">6.</span></span><span> XGBoost (Ensemble)

---

</span><span><span class="hljs-section">## Comparison Table</span></span><span>

Fill in the actual metric values after running the models.

| ML Model Name | Accuracy | AUC | Precision | Recall | F1 | MCC |
|---------------|----------|-----|-----------|--------|----|-----|
| Logistic Regression |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Decision Tree |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| kNN |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Naive Bayes |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Random Forest (Ensemble) |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| XGBoost (Ensemble) |  |  |  |  |  |  |

---

</span><span><span class="hljs-section">## Observations on Model Performance</span></span><span>

| ML Model Name | Observation about model performance |
|---------------|-------------------------------------|
| Logistic Regression | Performs well when classes are linearly separable; benefits from feature scaling. |
| Decision Tree | Can capture non-linear relationships but may overfit if not controlled. |
| kNN | Sensitive to scaling and high-dimensional data; performance depends on k value. |
| Naive Bayes | Fast baseline model; assumes feature independence; may underperform for complex patterns. |
| Random Forest (Ensemble) | Reduces overfitting compared to single tree; generally strong performance on tabular data. |
| XGBoost (Ensemble) | Often provides best performance on structured datasets with proper tuning. |

---

</span><span><span class="hljs-section">## How to Run</span></span><span>

</span><span><span class="hljs-section">### Run Individual Model Scripts</span></span><span>
<span class="hljs-code">```bash
python Logistic_Regression.py
python Decision_Tree.py
python KNN.py
python naive_bayes_gaussian.py
python random_forest_classifier.py
python xgboost_classifier.py
</span></span></span></code></div></div></pre>
<h3 data-start="3145" data-end="3166">Run Streamlit App</h3>
